The `shouldUseESMLoader()` function decides whether to use the ESM loader based on:\\n- The `--experimental-default-type=module` flag\\n- The presence of custom loaders via `--experimental-loader`\\n- The presence of preloaded modules via `--import`\\n- File extensions (.mjs vs .cjs)\\n- The `type` field in the nearest package.json\\n\\nOnce ESM loading is determined, `asyncRunEntryPointWithESMLoader()` invokes the cascaded loader through `lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js`.\\n\\n### Core Loader Architecture\\n\\n**ModuleLoader Class** (lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js, line 110) is the central component managing module loading. It maintains:\\n- `#resolveCache`: Registry of resolved specifiers using ResolveCache from module_map.js\\n- `loadCache`: Registry of loaded modules (ModuleJob instances)\\n- `translators`: ESM format translators from translators.js\\n- `#customizations`: Optional hooks customizations\\n\\nThe ModuleLoader provides:\\n- `async import()`: Dynamic module import\\n- `async resolve()`: Specifier resolution\\n- `resolveSync()`: Synchronous specifier resolution for import.meta.resolve\\n- `async load()`: Module loading and format detection\\n- `async eval()`: Direct source evaluation\\n- `getModuleJobForImport()`: Obtains or creates a ModuleJob for imports\\n\\n### Module Resolution Pipeline\\n\\nThe resolution process is implemented in `lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js`:\\n\\n1. **defaultResolve()** (line 1011): Main export resolver that:\\n   - Handles data: and node: URLs\\n   - Detects relative/absolute paths\\n   - Calls `moduleResolve()` for actual resolution\\n   - Returns format hints via `defaultGetFormatWithoutErrors()`\\n\\n2. **moduleResolve()** (line 899): Core algorithm that:\\n   - Handles built-in modules\\n   - Resolves package exports using `packageExportsResolve()`\\n   - Handles package imports via `packageImportsResolve()`\\n   - Supports legacy main resolution\\n\\n3. **packageExportsResolve()** and **packageImportsResolve()**: Implement package.json exports/imports field resolution per the Node.js specification.\\n\\n4. **decorateErrorWithCommonJSHints()** (line 1090): Attempts to provide helpful CommonJS alternatives when ESM resolution fails.\\n\\n### Format Detection and Loading\\n\\n**Module Format Detection** (lib/internal/modules/esm/get_format.js):\\n- `defaultGetFormat()`: Determines module format based on file extension, package.json type field, and MIME type\\n- Protocol-specific handlers in `protocolHandlers` for file:, data:, and node: URLs\\n- `detectModuleFormat()`: Uses the `containsModuleSyntax` binding to detect ambiguous files\\n\\n**defaultLoad()** and **defaultLoadSync()** (lib/internal/modules/esm/load.js, lines 87 and 158):\\n- Load source code from file:, data:, or node: URLs\\n- Validate import attributes\\n- Determine format if not provided\\n- Maintain backward compatibility for CommonJS\\n\\n### Module Translation\\n\\nThe **translators** map (lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js, line 81) provides format-specific handlers:\\n- `module`: JavaScript ES module translator using `compileSourceTextModule()`\\n- `commonjs`: CommonJS module translator using the CJS loader\\n- `json`: JSON module translator\\n- `wasm`: WebAssembly module translator\\n- `builtin`: Built-in module translator\\n\\nEach translator returns a ModuleWrap instance.\\n\\n### ModuleJob Linking and Evaluation Pipeline\\n\\nThe **ModuleJob** class (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js, line 72) tracks a single module's loading lifecycle:\\n\\n1. **Linking Phase** (`async _link()`, line 114):\\n   - Retrieves module requests from the ModuleWrap via `getModuleRequests()`\\n   - Recursively loads dependent modules via `loader.getModuleJobForImport()`\\n   - Calls `module.link()` on the native ModuleWrap with dependency modules\\n\\n2. **Instantiation Phase** (`async _instantiate()`, line 160):\\n   - Builds dependency graph of all modules\\n   - Calls `module.instantiate()` on the native ModuleWrap\\n   - Handles inspector breakpoint pausing if enabled\\n   - Provides helpful error messages for missing exports when importing from CommonJS\\n\\n3. **Evaluation Phase** (`async run()`, line 262):\\n   - Calls `module.evaluate()` on the native ModuleWrap\\n   - Handles top-level await and returns the module namespace\\n\\nThe related **ModuleJobSync** class (line 310) provides synchronous variants for use in CommonJS require() resolution.\\n\\n### ModuleWrap C++ Binding\\n\\nThe native **ModuleWrap** class (src/module_wrap.h and src/module_wrap.cc) wraps V8's Module object:\\n\\n**Key Methods**:\\n- `Link()`: Connects module dependencies\\n- `Instantiate()`: Instantiates the V8 module and its dependencies\\n- `Evaluate()`: Executes the module code\\n- `GetNamespace()`: Returns the module's export namespace\\n- `GetModuleRequests()`: Retrieves import/require specifiers\\n-
